I especially like the cleaners on the 19th floor, who are polite, diligent, serious and well-educated. The breakfast on the fifth floor of the hotel is rich, and the seafood noodles are particularly delicious and unforgettable. The dishes in the Chinese restaurant on the second floor are very good, with rich seafood, and the seafood pot is worth recommending. Guests staying in the hotel enjoy discounts when dining and checking out, which is very friendly and warm. The hotel is in a superior geographical location, right by the sea, and it is very convenient to see the sea view. It is also close to the World Style Street. A few dozen meters away is the "Ho Chi Minh Trail on the Sea". In order to resist the United States and aid Vietnam, my country built a hidden maritime transport route in 1968. The starting point is in Fangchenggang City and the end point is Haiphong City in Vietnam. This route is known as the "Ho Chi Minh Trail on the Sea" and is code-named "Guangxi 3¬∑22 Project". The hotel is cost-effective and sincerely recommended.

posted:Posted January 23, 2024
msg:I have been to Fangchenggang several times, and I stayed here every time. I came here before the epidemic, and it was summer. This is the first time I came in winter. Because the wind is very strong at the seaside, and the temperature has dropped in a large area these days, it is so cold. This time I feel that their management is much better than before, and the employees are not lazy. They will also take the initiative to help the guests. In general, they are more flexible than before and know how to adapt. When I came, it was the last high-speed rail to arrive. It was almost 9 o'clock and 10 o'clock. The front desk quickly checked in and upgraded the sea view room. It was also very warm to inform that because the wind is strong at the seaside, the sound of the wind may be very loud, but don't worry. The room 2026 I stayed in was very large, but I don't know if it was because it was at the seaside. There was a damp and musty smell. I contacted the front desk and quickly asked the staff to take me to another room. After that, I changed to Room 2021, which is close to the pedestrian street and there is no damp smell. I am very satisfied with the handling of the staff. Next is the restaurant. I didn't feel like I had any experience with breakfast before, but this time, there are so many types of breakfast. Their seafood porridge and seafood noodles are delicious, and there are also many snacks such as bread and cakes. If you want to eat good meals, you have to choose a hotel like this. Now there are many chain restaurants on the market that can only be said to be filling and mediocre. Although the hotel facilities are old, the service of the staff is better than before, and the food is delicious. I will continue to choose this place next time. Finally, I still have to give a suggestion. I hope the hotel can deal with the damp smell near the sea in time. Other than that, everything is good~
